<script>
	const popupOverlay = document.getElementById('customPopupOverlay');
    const closeButton = document.getElementById('customPopupClose');
    const popupForm = document.getElementById('customPopupForm');

    function showPopup() {
      if (popupOverlay) {
        popupOverlay.classList.add('visible');
      }
    }

    function hidePopup() {
		setCookie('popupDismissed', 'true', 1);
      if (popupOverlay) {
        popupOverlay.classList.remove('visible');
      }
		
    }
	function setCookie(name, value, days) {
    let expires = "";
    if (days) {
      const date = new Date();
      date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
      expires = "; expires=" + date.toUTCString();
    }
    document.cookie = name + "=" + (value || "") + expires + "; path=/";
  }

  // Belirtilen isme sahip çerezi getiren fonksiyon
  function getCookie(name) {
    const nameEQ = name + "=";
    const ca = document.cookie.split(';');
    for (let i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
      let c = ca[i];
      while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
      if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
    }
    return null;
  }
